The room is large. Although it is a bit old, it is well maintained. The room matches the picture.

The service is particularly impressive. When you enter the door and walk on the road, all the staff greet you warmly, and there is a special person to consult about the boat ride to the island. The service is proactive and enthusiastic, making this vacation very worry-free and smooth.
Reservations usually come with breakfast. The buffet restaurant on the 3rd floor can see the core landscape of the central lake area, which is the same as the central lake view room.
